				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Symphony No.9 in D minor, WAB 109 (Bruckner, Anton)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>3 movements
<dl><dd>I. Feierlich, misterioso
</dd><dd>II. Scherzo. Bewegt, lebhaft; Trio. Schnell
</dd><dd>III. Adagio. Langsam, feierlich
</dd><dd> <i>Finale (incomplete)</i>. Misterioso, nicht schnell
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1894 (movements 1-3); 1895-05-24 to 1896 (Finale)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Symphonies&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Symphonies</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_orchestra&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For orchestra</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_orchestra&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the orchestra</a></span>; <span class="expandline" title="7 more..."><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_2_pianos_%28arr%29&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For 2 pianos (arr)</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_piano&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the piano</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_2_players&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For 2 players</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_piano_4_hands_%28arr%29&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For piano 4 hands (arr)</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_piano_4_hands&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the piano 4 hands</a></span>; <th>Misc. Notes
</th>
<td>ca.320dpi color images. This file is based on high-resolution images obtained from the source using a method explained on <a href="/wiki/IMSLP:Obtaining_High-Resolution_Images" title="IMSLP:Obtaining High-Resolution Images">this page</a>. Composer autograph manuscript with additional markings. Pages 81 and 105 on Bruckner Online was blank when downloading but on the <i>Österreichische Nationalbibliothek</i>, they had the pages that showed up to download from correctly. Replaced the blank page from Bruckner Online with the <i>Österreichische Nationalbibliothek</i> one. Hopefully Bruckner Online will correct the image download error on there site. Taken from Bruckner Online: <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.bruckner-online.at/ID102">Mus.Hs.6087</a></span>.
</td></tr>

</li><li>First Trio (F major, 1889) and second Trio (F-sharp major, 1893): <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.dra.de/online/dokument/2008/dok2008-1.html">Die Trio-Entwürfe zum 2. Satz der 9. Sinfonie von Anton Bruckner</a> by the Strub-Quartett (1940)
</li><li>Finale completions:

<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>

<td>3 movements
<dl><dd>I. Feierlich, misterioso
</dd><dd>II. Scherzo. Bewegt, lebhaft; Trio. Schnell
</dd><dd>III. Adagio. Langsam, feierlich
</dd><dd> <i>Finale (incomplete)</i>. Misterioso, nicht schnell
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1894 (movements 1-3); 1895-05-24 to 1896 (Finale)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>

<td>1903 February 11 or earlier
<dl><dd>See <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.wienersymphoniker.at/archiv/concert/pid/000000e9h58h0000fd40">Vienna Symphony Archives</a></span>
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>

</td></tr>
<tr>

<td><i>Orchestra:</i> 3 flutes/piccolo, 3 oboes, 3 clarinets (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>/A), 3 bassoons<br />8 horns in F (horns 5-6 also Wagner tubas in B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>, horns 7-8 also Wagner tubas in F),<br />3 trumpets (F), 3 trombones, tuba + timpani + strings

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<ul><li>First performance in France (or Paris? unclear from text) may have been 16 December 1906? (See <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=geYEAAAAMAAJ&amp;pg=PA792"><i>Le Guide Musical</i></a></span> (December 9 1906 issue, list of concerts, with an article, by May de Rudder, about the soon to be performed symphony starting <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=geYEAAAAMAAJ&amp;pg=PA779">here</a></span>.))
</li><li>The 1894 version is the <b>Original version</b>. The 1st published version (1903) is an <i><b>apocryphal</b></i> version, in which Bruckner's pupil, Ferdinand Löwe introduced a lot of unauthorized changes. See <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.bruckner.webs.com/versions.html#sym9">Bruckner's Symphony No. 9 versions by David Griegel</a>.
</li></ul>
